During the game a player may add to their own spread, or an opponent’s spread. Play ends when a player has no cards left.\r\n\r\nTonk is played by 2 or 3 players. The dealer deals five cards face down, and one at a time to each player in a clockwise direction. The rest of the cards are stacked and kept in the center as the draw pile.
